## SECTION 27 — ACQUISITION ATTRACTIVENESS

### Likely Buyers & Strategic Rationale

| Buyer | Interest | Why | Valuation Range |
|-------|----------|-----|-----------------|
| **Twilio** | VERY HIGH | Voice + comms layer + SMB distribution | $150M–$400M |
| **HubSpot** | VERY HIGH | SMB revenue tools, follow-up automation, CRM adjacency | $200M–$500M |
| **ServiceTitan** | HIGH | Home services vertical domination, recurring revenue, agency channel | $100M–$300M |
| **Toast** | HIGH | Restaurant/service vertical, POS integration, recurring revenue | $80M–$250M |
| **Salesforce** | MEDIUM | Revenue cloud strategy, SMB expansion, enterprise credibility | $300M–$1B |
| **Private Equity** | MEDIUM | Platform play (20%+ margins, recurring, scalable model) | $150M–$400M |
| **HubSpot Competitor** | MEDIUM | Pipedrive, Zoho could acquire for feature parity | $80M–$200M |

### What Acquirers Value

**Quantifiable Assets:**
1. **Customer Base:**
   - 4,000–6,000 SMB customers (recurring, sticky, high LTV)
   - 50–100 enterprise customers (strategic anchors)
   - Geographic diversity reduces risk
   - Vertical concentration (HVAC, dental, legal, sales) shows expertise

2. **Unit Economics:**
   - LTV:CAC ratio >3:1 (proven efficient acquisition)
   - CAC payback <6 months (low cash burn, fast scaling)
   - Gross margin >80% (high-quality SaaS business)
   - NRR >115% (expansion revenue potential)
   - Churn <4% SMB (retention excellence)

3. **Revenue & Growth:**
   - $5M–$10M ARR at 30–50% YoY growth
   - MRR growth trajectory ($150K→$500K+ MRR)
   - Predictable monthly revenue (no one-off deals)

4. **Product Defensibility:**
   - Proprietary voice stack (self-hosted, cost moat)
   - Contact memory graph (data moat)
   - Industry template library (vertical expertise)
   - Integration depth (CRM, calendar, phone)

5. **Data Assets (Increasingly Valuable):**
   - Call patterns by industry (follow-up timing optimal for conversions)
   - Conversion benchmarks (e.g., "HVAC follow-up within 2 hours = 35% conversion")
   - Contact behavior graphs (preferences, communication style, success history)
   - Aggregated insights (20M+ call interactions, anonymized)

6. **Strategic Positioning:**
   - Category ownership: "Recall Touch = follow-up OS"
   - Vertical dominance in 3–5 high-value segments
   - Agency ecosystem (50–100 partners, 30–40% of revenue)
   - Brand equity in SMB/service business space

### Buyer-Specific Analysis

**Twilio (Most Likely Buyer: Month 24–36)**
- **Why:** Twilio owns voice/SMS infrastructure; Recall Touch is best-in-class customer
- **Fit:** Adding revenue recovery product layer increases ARPU, cross-sell into 100K+ Twilio customers
- **Valuation:** $200M–$400M (6–8x revenue multiple, standard for SaaS platform acquires)
- **Integration:** Stripe Recall Touch branding into Twilio Console; offer to Twilio customers as white-label
- **Synergies:** Eliminate Twilio infrastructure costs (pass through to margin), cross-sell, data insights

**HubSpot (High Likelihood: Month 24–36)**
- **Why:** HubSpot wants SMB revenue tools (sales, marketing, service); Recall Touch adds omnichannel follow-up
- **Fit:** Integrate into HubSpot Hub (same way they bought Breeze for email, GloCap for video)
- **Valuation:** $250M–$500M (8–10x revenue, premium for strategic fit)
- **Integration:** Recall Touch becomes HubSpot Sales Hub feature; contact memory trained on HubSpot data
- **Synergies:** Upsell to 100K+ HubSpot customers, eliminate vendor costs, deepen SMB stickiness

**ServiceTitan (Medium-High Likelihood: Month 24–36)**
- **Why:** ServiceTitan owns home services vertical (HVAC, plumbing, electrical); Recall Touch owns follow-up in that space
- **Fit:** Vertical integration; customer can't escape ServiceTitan ecosystem
- **Valuation:** $100M–$300M (5–7x revenue, lower due to more niche fit)
- **Integration:** Deep POS/dispatch integration; dispatch system triggers Recall Touch follow-up
- **Synergies:** Lock-in customers, reduce churn, increase ARPU within vertical

**Salesforce (Lower Likelihood: Post-$20M ARR)**
- **Why:** Salesforce Revenue Cloud strategy (Einstein + automation + engagement)
- **Fit:** Recall Touch = engagement layer on top of Salesforce CRM
- **Valuation:** $300M–$1B+ (7–10x revenue, but Salesforce pays premium for strategic fit)
- **Integration:** Embed Recall Touch into Salesforce; Einstein AI absorbs contact memory
- **Synergies:** De-commoditize Salesforce for SMB; add engagement layer competitors don't have

### Metrics That Drive Valuation

| Metric | Target (Acquisition Readiness) | Impact on Valuation |
|--------|------------------------------|-------------------|
| ARR | $5M–$10M | Base for multiple (6–10x) |
| YoY Growth | 30–50% | +1–2x multiple (growth premium) |
| Gross Margin | 80%+ | +0.5–1x multiple (quality of revenue) |
| NRR | 115%+ | +1–2x multiple (expansion potential) |
| Churn | <3% | +0.5–1x multiple (retention excellence) |
| CAC Payback | <5 months | +0.5x multiple (efficiency signal) |
| Market Share | Top 3 in category | +1–2x multiple (defensibility) |
| Logo Retention | >90% | +0.5–1x multiple (customer satisfaction) |

**Valuation Formula (Illustrative):**
- Base multiple: 6x ARR ($10M × 6 = $60M)
- Growth premium (40% YoY): +2x ($20M)
- Margin premium (82% GM): +1x ($10M)
- Retention premium (NRR 118%): +1x ($10M)
- Category premium (market leader): +1x ($10M)
- **Total: $110M–$200M valuation**

*Note: Strategic acquirers (HubSpot, Twilio) often pay 8–12x multiples; financial buyers (PE) pay 5–7x.*

### Building Toward $100M+ Standalone AND $100M+ Acquisition

**The Balanced Path (Play Both Sides):**

1. **Months 0–12: Prove SMB Unit Economics**
   - Path to $1M ARR; clean metrics that show acquirer confidence
   - Attractive to acquirers; also shows path to independence

2. **Months 12–24: Category Leadership + Agency Moat**
   - Build defensible moats (contact memory, voice, agency network)
   - Makes you valuable as acquisition (data, ecosystem, stickiness)
   - Also positions you for $10M+ ARR independently

3. **Months 24–36: Enterprise Motion + Acquisition Conversations**
   - If acquisition offer >$100M at month 24–30, take it (95% of founders should)
   - If not, build enterprise customers to $5M–$10M ARR, then re-engage buyers
   - Building enterprise (not replacing SMB) = compatible with both paths

4. **Months 36+: $100M+ Standalone**
   - If you reach $10M ARR + clear path to $20M, acquisition interest becomes irrelevant
   - You can either sell for $200M–$500M, or stay independent and scale to $100M+

**Key Insight:** Avoid building specifically "for acquisition" (weakens unit economics). Build for profitability and dominance. Acquisition comes naturally.

---

## SECTION 28 — FINAL DECISION STACK

### 10 Core Decisions

**1. Category Definition (Strategic Positioning)**
- **Decision:** Positioning as "Revenue Execution OS" (not "follow-up platform" or "AI assistant")
- **Why:** Broader than follow-up (includes booking, sequences, accountability). Premium feel. Enterprise credible. Defensible category.
- **Messaging:** "Every call, conversation, and opportunity—never lost again."
- **Timeline:** Communicate in homepage redesign (Day 1); all marketing materials (Week 2)

**2. Initial Wedge (Go-to-Market Focus)**
- **Decision:** Service businesses losing money to missed calls (dental, HVAC, legal intake, coaching)
- **Why:**
  - Highest revenue-per-call ($100–$1,000), so ROI messaging works (recover $500–$5K/month)
  - Pain is acute and quantifiable ("3 missed calls today = $2,100 lost")
  - Less competitive (Salesforce/HubSpot don't focus here)
  - Fastest to PMF (12–16 weeks to 30–50 customers)
- **Secondary wedge (Month 6):** Sales teams with high call volume (SMB SaaS, staffing, insurance)
- **Timeline:** Founder-led sales + case studies (Months 1–3); scale via agencies and content (Months 4–12)

**3. Broad-Market Positioning (Long-Term Framing)**
- **Decision:** "Every missed call, forgotten follow-up, and lost opportunity — recovered automatically."
- **Why:** Speaks to emotional pain (loss) + functional benefit (automation) + outcome (recovery)
- **Audience:** Primarily SMB owners, sales leaders, service business owners
- **Timeline:** Finalize in brand guide (Month 1); use in all marketing, sales, product content

**4. Homepage Message (Immediate Priority)**
- **Decision:** "Stop Losing Revenue to Missed Follow-Ups"
- **Alternative options considered (rejected):**
  - "AI-Powered Follow-Up Automation" (too generic, commoditized)
  - "The Follow-Up OS" (too technical)
  - "Never Miss a Booking Again" (too narrow)
- **Why this wins:** Speaks to pain (loss of revenue), specific pain (follow-ups), urgency (now)
- **Subcopy:** "Recover missed calls, auto-follow-up with leads, book appointments — without lifting a finger."
- **CTA:** "Start free trial (14 days, no credit card)"
- **Timeline:** Homepage redesign complete by Day 7

**5. Pricing Strategy (Revenue Model)**
- **Decision:** Tiered by outcome/complexity, not seats
  - **Solo:** $29/month (1 person, <100 calls/month) — for solopreneurs, small service businesses
  - **Starter:** $79/month (2–5 people, 100–500 calls/month) — SMB service businesses
  - **Growth:** $199/month (5–20 people, 500–2K calls/month) — growing SMB + sales teams
  - **Scale:** $499/month (20+ people, 2K+ calls/month) — mid-market
  - **Enterprise:** Custom (100+ users, compliance, custom voice, integrations)

- **Why this works:**
  - Outcome-based (revenue recovery) not features-based (seats)
  - Encourages expansion (add people = upgrade tier)
  - Defensible against price compression (each tier serves distinct segment)
  - Gross margin targets: Solo 75%, Starter 82%, Growth 84%, Scale 85%, Enterprise 86%

- **Pricing logic:**
  - Solo: Low ARPU, high churn; acceptable loss for brand
  - Starter: Goldilocks zone; focus optimization here
  - Growth: Premium segment; 15–20% margin expansion
  - Scale: Enterprise-adjacent; margin focused
  - Enterprise: LTV$318K+; custom pricing justified

- **Timeline:** Pricing page live (Month 1); test and optimize through Month 6; lock in by Month 6

**6. Margin Protection Move (Cost Optimization)**
- **Decision:** Self-hosted voice stack to eliminate per-minute vendor dependency
  - **Current cost:** ElevenLabs $0.10/min; Twilio $0.05/min = $0.15/min
  - **Target cost:** Self-hosted TTS $0.001/min (100x reduction)
  - **Margin impact:** 4–8% ARPU improvement (highest ROI engineering project)

- **Implementation path:**
  - Month 3: Evaluate Coqui, Meta Voicebox, Google TTS
  - Month 6: Self-hosted voice v1 (80% quality parity, <$1K/month cost)
  - Month 12: 90%+ quality parity, rolled out to 80% of new customers
  - Month 18: Deprecated ElevenLabs for standard calls; available only for premium voice cloning

- **Why this matters:** Differentiates from competitors who rely on API costs. Enables aggressive SMB pricing without margin compression.

**7. Strongest Moat-Building Move (Long-Term Defensibility)**
- **Decision:** Triple-layered moat:
  1. **Contact Memory Graph** (12–24 months): AI learns each contact's communication preferences, history, optimal timing. Switching cost = losing 6+ months of behavioral data.
  2. **Industry Benchmark Data** (12–24 months): Publish annual reports on follow-up effectiveness by industry. Positioning = "data-driven follow-up."
  3. **Agency Distribution Network** (6–24 months): 100+ agencies building customer businesses on top. Network effect: more agencies = more customers = more agencies want to join.

- **Why all three together:** Single moat is fragile. Three combined are very strong:
  - Data moat requires design (intentional, feeds back to product)
  - Workflow moat (sequences) is replicable; contact memory is not
  - Agency moat creates distribution that competitors can't replicate without spending 5 years

- **Timeline:** Contact memory v1 by Month 6, v2+ by Month 12. First benchmark report Month 12. First 10 agencies Month 6, 100 agencies by Month 24.

**8. Biggest Mistake to Avoid (Anti-Pattern)**
- **Decision:** Do NOT try to be a CRM or "all-in-one sales tool"
  - **Why:** Impossible to compete with HubSpot/Salesforce
  - **Symptom of drift:** "We should add lead database," "We should have contact management," "We should have pipelines"
  - **Correction:** Every request gets filtered through: "Does this improve follow-up recovery specifically?" If no, defer or integrate instead of build
  - **Principle:** Be 10x better at one thing (follow-up recovery) rather than 10% better at 10 things

- **How to enforce:**
  - Quarterly product review: "What % of engineering went to core follow-up vs. peripheral features?" Target: 80% core / 20% supporting
  - Hiring: Every hire must improve follow-up recovery or unit economics (no pure "full-stack engineers building random features")
  - Roadmap: No quarter should have >3 projects that aren't core to follow-up recovery

**9. Clearest Path to 9 Figures (Scaling Model)**
- **Decision:** Phased geographic & segment expansion:
  - **Phase 1 (Year 1):** Dominate SMB service businesses in US (dental, HVAC, legal, coaching, cleaning)
    - Target: 2,000–3,000 customers, $1M–$2M ARR
    - Methods: Founder sales, content, agencies
  - **Phase 2 (Year 2):** Expand to sales teams (SaaS, insurance, staffing, recruiting)
    - Target: +2,000 sales team customers, $3M–$5M ARR
  - **Phase 3 (Year 2–3):** Layer in enterprise (HubSpot, Salesforce, custom)
    - Target: +100 enterprise customers, $5M–$10M ARR
  - **Phase 4 (Year 3+):** Agency channel scales (50–100 agencies)
    - Target: 40% of new customers sourced through agencies, $10M–$25M ARR
  - **Phase 5 (Year 3–4):** International expansion (UK, Australia, Canada)
    - Target: +$5M–$10M ARR from English-speaking markets

- **Why this order works:**
  - Each phase builds on previous (not competing for engineering)
  - Service businesses → sales teams (same core product, different verticals)
  - Enterprise comes after SMB is proven (de-risks enterprise motion)
  - Agency channel scales only after 3,000+ customers (network effects kick in)
  - International is last (lowest strategic ROI until $10M+ ARR)

**10. Final Product Shape (Definition at Maturity)**
- **Decision:** "AI-Powered Follow-Up and Revenue Recovery OS with Voice, Omnichannel Sequences, Booking, and Industry Playbooks"
  - **Core:** Captures missed calls, auto-triggers follow-up sequences
  - **Sequences:** Multi-channel (call, SMS, email), conditional logic, approval workflows
  - **Voice:** Self-hosted TTS, custom cloning for enterprise, voice marketplace
  - **Booking:** Embedded calendly-style booking, integrations with Calendly/Acuity
  - **Verticals:** Industry-specific playbooks, templates, benchmarks (dental, HVAC, sales, etc.)
  - **Integrations:** HubSpot, Salesforce, Calendly, Google Calendar, Outlook, Stripe, Zapier
  - **Intelligence:** Contact memory, optimal timing recommendations, churn prediction, ROI analytics
  - **Team:** Multi-user, manager oversight, approval workflows, audit logs
  - **Trust:** Transparent AI, human-in-loop approvals, TCPA compliance, SOC 2/HIPAA roadmap

- **What it's NOT:**
  - Not a CRM (no contact database as core; integrates with existing CRM)
  - Not a chatbot (no text-based chat; voice-first for missed calls)
  - Not a social media tool
  - Not a generic automation platform (focused on revenue recovery specifically)

- **Timeline:** Core defined by Month 3. Added to product messaging by Month 6. Fully built by Month 24.

---

## FINAL SYNTHESIS: Strategic Thesis

**Recall Touch is building the operating system for revenue recovery in the SMB market.**

The thesis:
1. **Pain:** Businesses lose 15–35% of potential revenue to missed calls, forgotten follow-ups, and delayed responses.
2. **Solution:** AI automates follow-up across voice, SMS, email, and booking—without lost context or quality.
3. **Market:** 5 million SMBs in service (dental, HVAC, legal, coaching) + sales teams (SaaS, insurance, staffing) = $10B+ TAM.
4. **Positioning:** Own "follow-up and revenue recovery" category. Be to follow-up what Slack is to team communication.
5. **Economics:** SMB segment has 11:1 LTV:CAC, 8-month payback, 4% churn, 82% gross margin. Sustainable path to $100M+ ARR.
6. **Moats:** Contact memory (non-exportable data), industry benchmarks (exclusive insights), agency ecosystem (distribution), voice technology (margin protection).
7. **Acquisition Path:** Either $100M–$500M acquisition (Twilio, HubSpot) by year 3, or $100M+ standalone ARR by year 4.
8. **Key Insight:** Don't try to be a CRM. Be 10x better at one thing. Follow-up recovery is the wedge that unlocks everything else.

**This is a $100M+ company if executed with focus and discipline.**



---

# PART II: IMPLEMENTATION BRIEF FOR CURSOR

# RECALL TOUCH MASTER STRATEGY V5
## IMPLEMENTATION BRIEF FOR CURSOR

---

## PART 1 — PRODUCT SURFACES

### Shared Surfaces (All Modes)
- **Navigation Bar**: Logo, mode switcher, workspace selector, notification bell, user profile dropdown, help/docs
- **Search**: Global command palette (Cmd+K), contact search, conversation search, template search
- **Settings**: Organization settings, team management, integrations, billing, security, preferences
- **Help & Onboarding**: In-app tours, tooltip system, docs link, support chat, video guides

### Solo Mode Surfaces
- **Dashboard**: Single KPI panel (calls booked today, pipeline value, revenue), quick-action buttons (New Contact, Start Conversation, View Inbox)
- **Inbox**: Unified conversation stream (voicemail + SMS + AI responses), sort by recency/priority, mark complete
- **Contacts**: Simple list/card view, import CSV, manual add, notes per contact, last interaction date
- **Call History**: Call log with duration/outcome/recording, transcription preview, bulk export
- **Quick Sequences**: Pre-built templates, drag-drop editor, one-click deploy to contact
- **Billing Lite**: Current plan, usage this month (calls, SMS, AI responses), upgrade button

### Sales Mode Surfaces
- **Dashboard**: Leads by stage, pipeline value, calls booked, conversion rate, daily quota progress, team leaderboard (if team_id set)
- **Opportunity Board**: Kanban view of opportunities by stage, bulk move, add notes, assign follow-ups, revenue visualization
- **Contact Timeline**: Full history (calls, meetings, emails, notes, tasks), add event, log call outcome
- **Inbox Pro**: Conversation routing by VCN, priority scoring (high-intent keywords), unread count per rep
- **Workflow Builder**: Visual sequence editor, conditions (stage match, tag, date), actions (call, SMS, task, email), scheduling
- **Sequences**: Saved sequences, copy/customize, A/B testing view, send history, response rates
- **Reporting**: Conversion by rep, pipeline velocity, no-show recovery rate, missed-call recovery rate, forecast
- **Team**: Team members, activity log, rep assignments, performance rankings

### Business Mode Surfaces
- **Workspace Dashboard**: Multi-org/location KPIs, top performers, revenue by location, team health
- **Organization Admin**: Org settings, locations, roles, permissions matrix, team structure
- **Advanced Workflows**: Multi-trigger, multi-condition, routing rules (lead scoring, geographic), API integrations
- **Sequence Library**: Organization-wide library, version control, usage by location, A/B variants
- **Analytics Suite**: Cohort analysis, funnel analysis, attribution, predictive churn, industry benchmarking
- **Voice Library**: Voice profiles, voice versions, pronunciation rules, voice quality metrics, custom voice management
- **Team Admin**: Bulk user management, role assignment, location assignment, activity audit, cost allocation
- **Billing Admin**: Department/location cost allocation, margin monitoring, custom contracts, invoice export
- **Integrations Hub**: CRM sync (Salesforce, HubSpot, Pipedrive), Slack, Zapier, custom webhooks, data sync status
- **Industry Packs**: Select industry template, adapt contact fields, customize sequences, use industry voice library

### Shared Admin Surfaces
- **Audit Log**: All user actions (login, create/edit/delete, permission change), timestamp, actor, IP
- **Security**: API keys, webhook management, IP whitelist, session management, 2FA setup
- **Voice Preferences**: Default voice profile, fallback voice, voice consent settings, voice usage limits
- **Notification Preferences**: Email alerts (team activity, billing), SMS alerts (critical), in-app banner settings
- **Data Export**: GDPR export, bulk contact export, conversation export, call recording archive

---

## PART 2 — CORE DATA MODEL

### Core Entities (Supabase revenue_operator schema)

**users**
- id (uuid, pk)
- email (text, unique)
- full_name (text)
- password_hash (text, encrypted)
- workspace_id (fk → organizations)
- role_id (fk → roles)
- is_active (boolean, default true)
- is_verified_email (boolean)
- phone (text, optional)
- timezone (text, default 'UTC')
- preferences (jsonb: theme, notification_level, language, sidebar_collapse)
- profile_image_url (text, optional)
- last_login_at (timestamp)
- created_at (timestamp)
- updated_at (timestamp)
- RLS: users can read/write own row; managers can read team rows; admins full access

**organizations**
- id (uuid, pk)
- name (text)
- slug (text, unique)
- logo_url (text, optional)
- industry (enum: real_estate, insurance, automotive, healthcare, finance, saas, other)
- plan_id (fk → billing_plans)
- billing_contact_id (fk → users)
- is_active (boolean)
- stripe_customer_id (text, unique, nullable)
- stripe_subscription_id (text, nullable)
- subscription_status (enum: trial, active, paused, canceled, past_due)
- trial_started_at (timestamp, nullable)
- trial_days_remaining (integer, default 14)
- billing_email (text)
- billing_address (jsonb)
- annual_contract_value (numeric, nullable)
- currency (text, default 'USD')
- metadata (jsonb: white_label_settings, partner_code, cost_limits)
- created_at (timestamp)
- updated_at (timestamp)
- RLS: org members can read own org; only admins can update settings

**teams**
- id (uuid, pk)
- organization_id (fk → organizations)
- name (text)
- description (text, optional)
- is_active (boolean, default true)
- manager_id (fk → users, optional)
- cost_center_code (text, optional)
- location_id (fk → locations, optional)
- created_at (timestamp)
- updated_at (timestamp)
- RLS: team members can read own team; managers/admins can modify

**roles**
- id (uuid, pk)
- organization_id (fk → organizations)
- name (text: Admin, Manager, Sales Rep, Analyst, Viewer)
- description (text)
- is_system_role (boolean)
- permissions (text array: [contact.view, contact.create, contact.edit, contact.delete, workflow.view, workflow.create, workflow.execute, report.view, billing.view, billing.manage, team.manage, integration.view, integration.manage, voice.manage])
- created_at (timestamp)
- RLS: only admins can create/edit

**contacts**
- id (uuid, pk)
- organization_id (fk → organizations)
- team_id (fk → teams, optional)
- first_name (text)
- last_name (text)
- email (text, optional)
- phone (text, required for recall)
- secondary_phone (text, optional)
- company_name (text, optional)
- job_title (text, optional)
- industry (text, optional)
- source (enum: manual, import, api, facebook, linkedin, crm_sync)
- vcn (text, optional: Verifiable Caller Network ID)
- status (enum: active, archived, do_not_call)
- tags (text array)
- custom_fields (jsonb: extensible by industry/org)
- notes (text)
- last_interaction_date (timestamp)
- assigned_user_id (fk → users, optional)
- assigned_team_id (fk → teams, optional)
- preferred_contact_method (enum: call, sms, email)
- preferred_contact_window (jsonb: start_hour, end_hour, timezone)
- do_not_contact_until (timestamp, optional)
- consent_status (enum: opted_in, opted_out, pending_consent)
- consent_sources (text array: [sms_opt_in, voice_opt_in, email_opt_in])
- voice_profile_id (fk → voice_profiles, optional: preferred voice for this contact)
- created_at (timestamp)
- updated_at (timestamp)
- RLS: users can read contacts assigned to them or their team; admins full access

**conversations**
- id (uuid, pk)
- organization_id (fk → organizations)
- contact_id (fk → contacts)
- team_id (fk → teams, optional)
- channel (enum: voice_call, sms, email, voicemail, ai_response)
- direction (enum: inbound, outbound)
- status (enum: active, completed, missed, no_show, archived)
- initiator (enum: contact, system, user)
- initiator_user_id (fk → users, optional)
- ai_agent_id (text, optional)
- transcript (text, optional)
- transcription_status (enum: pending, completed, failed)
- duration_seconds (integer, optional)
- recording_url (text, optional)
- recording_status (enum: pending, ready, deleted)
- call_sid (text, unique, optional: Twilio SID)
- message_sid (text, unique, optional: Twilio SID)
- sentiment_score (numeric -1 to 1, optional)
- intent_detected (text array, optional: [interested, objection, follow_up_needed, not_interested])
- outcome (enum: booking, callback_scheduled, follow_up_scheduled, no_action, declined, interested, not_qualified)
- next_action_due (timestamp, optional)
- next_action_type (enum: call, sms, email, task, sequence_trigger)
- custom_fields (jsonb)
- started_at (timestamp)
- ended_at (timestamp, optional)
- created_at (timestamp)
- updated_at (timestamp)
- RLS: users can read conversations for contacts assigned to them; admins full access

**events**
- id (uuid, pk)
- organization_id (fk → organizations)
- contact_id (fk → contacts)
- conversation_id (fk → conversations, nullable)
- created_by_user_id (fk → users)
- event_type (enum: call_completed, call_missed, callback_scheduled, appointment_booked, appointment_no_show, follow_up_created, note_added, status_changed, sequence_started, sequence_completed, reminder_triggered, conversion, revenue_logged)
- event_name (text: human-readable label)
- metadata (jsonb: call_duration, appointment_date, appointment_value, stage_before, stage_after, reason, revenue_amount, revenue_currency, recovery_win_value)
- triggered_at (timestamp)
- created_at (timestamp)
- RLS: users can read events for own contacts; admins full access

**opportunities**
- id (uuid, pk)
- organization_id (fk → organizations)
- contact_id (fk → contacts)
- team_id (fk → teams, optional)
- name (text)
- stage (enum: initial_contact, qualified, proposal, negotiation, won, lost, archived)
- value (numeric)
- currency (text, default 'USD')
- probability (integer 0-100, optional: for forecast)
- estimated_close_date (date, optional)
- close_date (date, optional)
- reason_lost (text, optional)
- source_sequence_id (fk → sequences, optional)
- assigned_user_id (fk → users)
- custom_fields (jsonb)
- created_at (timestamp)
- updated_at (timestamp)
- RLS: users can read opportunities assigned to them; admins full access

**tasks**
- id (uuid, pk)
- organization_id (fk → organizations)
- contact_id (fk → contacts, optional)
- opportunity_id (fk → opportunities, optional)
- conversation_id (fk → conversations, optional)
- created_by_user_id (fk → users)
- assigned_user_id (fk → users)
- title (text)
- description (text)
- status (enum: open, in_progress, completed, archived)
- priority (enum: low, medium, high, urgent)
- due_date (timestamp)
- completed_at (timestamp, nullable)
- custom_fields (jsonb)
- created_at (timestamp)
- updated_at (timestamp)
- RLS: users can read/write tasks assigned to them; admins full access

**workflows**
- id (uuid, pk)
- organization_id (fk → organizations)
- team_id (fk → teams, optional)
- name (text)
- description (text)
- is_active (boolean, default true)
- trigger_type (enum: manual, conversation_outcome, event, scheduled, webhook, crm_event, sequence_enrollment)
- trigger_conditions (jsonb: conversation_status, intent_detected, contact_tags, time_range, crm_field_match)
- actions (jsonb array: [{type: call|sms|email|task|opportunity_update|webhook, config: {...}}])
- execution_order (enum: sequential, parallel)
- rate_limit (integer, optional: max executions per contact per day)
- error_handling (enum: retry, skip, notify)
- created_by_user_id (fk → users)
- last_updated_by_user_id (fk → users)
- version (integer, default 1)
- published_at (timestamp, nullable)
- created_at (timestamp)
- updated_at (timestamp)
- RLS: team members can view; managers can create/edit; admins full access

**sequences**
- id (uuid, pk)
- organization_id (fk → organizations)
- team_id (fk → teams, optional)
- name (text)
- description (text)
- category (enum: follow_up, nurture, objection_handler, closing, reactivation, industry_specific)
- is_active (boolean, default true)
- is_template (boolean)
- steps (jsonb array: [{step_number, action_type: call|sms|email, delay_hours, message_template_id, conditions}])
- success_criteria (enum: booking, response, call_completion, no_criteria)
- expected_conversion_rate (numeric, optional)
- version (integer)
- published_by_user_id (fk → users, nullable)
- published_at (timestamp, nullable)
- ab_test_variant_of (uuid, optional)
- ab_test_metrics (jsonb: variant_a_conversion, variant_b_conversion)
- created_at (timestamp)
- updated_at (timestamp)
- RLS: team members can read; managers can create/edit; admins full access

**sequence_enrollments**
- id (uuid, pk)
- sequence_id (fk → sequences)
- contact_id (fk → contacts)
- started_at (timestamp)
- status (enum: active, completed, paused, unsubscribed, bounced)
- current_step_number (integer)
- next_step_due_at (timestamp, nullable)
- completion_date (timestamp, nullable)
- last_step_completed_at (timestamp, nullable)
- conversions (integer array: step numbers that converted)
- created_at (timestamp)
- updated_at (timestamp)
- RLS: users can view enrollments for own contacts; admins full access

**templates**
- id (uuid, pk)
- organization_id (fk → organizations)
- template_type (enum: sms, email, voicemail, call_script)
- name (text)
- content (text: template with {{variable}} placeholders)
- variables (text array: [first_name, company_name, appointment_date, recovery_reason])
- category (enum: initial_outreach, follow_up, missed_call, no_show_recovery, appointment_confirmation)
- is_system_template (boolean)

- voice_profile_id (fk → voice_profiles, optional: for call scripts)

- created_by_user_id (fk → users)
- usage_count (integer, default 0)
- created_at (timestamp)
- updated_at (timestamp)
- RLS: users can view org templates; managers can create/edit; admins full access

**bookings**
- id (uuid, pk)

- scheduled_for (timestamp)
- duration_minutes (integer, default 30)
- location_id (fk → locations, optional)
- assigned_user_id (fk → users)
- status (enum: confirmed, rescheduled, no_show, completed, canceled)
- cancellation_reason (text, optional)

- notes (text, optional)
- custom_fields (jsonb)
- created_at (timestamp)
- updated_at (timestamp)
- RLS: users can read bookings assigned to them; admins full access

**reminders**
- id (uuid, pk)

- task_id (fk → tasks, optional)
- created_by_user_id (fk → users, optional)
- assigned_user_id (fk → users, optional)
- action_to_take (text)
- delivery_method (enum: sms, email, in_app, call)
- status (enum: pending, sent, completed, failed)
- sent_at (timestamp, nullable)
- attempts (integer, default 0)
- last_attempt_at (timestamp, nullable)
- created_at (timestamp)
- updated_at (timestamp)
- RLS: users can read reminders assigned to them; admins full access

**invoices**

- updated_at (timestamp)
- RLS: only org admins can view

**locations**
- id (uuid, pk)

- name (text)

- phone_number (text)

- RLS: org members can read; admins can manage

- RLS: org members can read; admins can create/edit

**quality_evaluation_records**

- audio_url (text)
- clarity_score (integer 1-10)

- word_error_rate (numeric, optional)

- RLS: admins and evaluators can read/write; org members can read

**voice_usage_records**
- id (uuid, pk)

**analytics_events**
- id (uuid, pk)
- organization_id (fk → organizations)
- event_category (enum: user_action, system_event, business_event, cost_event)
- event_name (text)
- event_properties (jsonb)
- timestamp (timestamp)
- RLS: only org admins can view

**audit_logs**
- id (uuid, pk)
- organization_id (fk → organizations)
- actor_user_id (fk → users)
- action (enum: create, read, update, delete, export, import, permission_change, role_change, api_call)
- resource_type (text: contacts, workflows, sequences, templates, users, organization_settings)
- resource_id (uuid, nullable)
- changes_before (jsonb, nullable)
- changes_after (jsonb, nullable)
- ip_address (text)
- user_agent (text)
- status (enum: success, failure)
- error_message (text, nullable)
- timestamp (timestamp)
- RLS: only org admins can view

---

## PART 3 — BACKEND / SYSTEM REQUIREMENTS

### Core Services & Subsystems

**Omnichannel Ingestion Layer**
- Inbound call handler (Twilio webhook): parse Call SID, phone, timestamp; route to contact lookup or create; trigger conversation record; dispatch to workflow engine
- Voicemail transcription handler: async job (Bull queue), call Faster-Whisper, store transcript, detect sentiment, trigger voicemail-specific workflows
- SMS inbound handler (Twilio): similar to call, store message, route to workflow
- Email integration handler (if Zapier/IFTTT bridge): receive webhook, parse subject/body, create conversation, route to workflow
- Outbound call initiator (Twilio): accept workflow action, validate contact consent, provision Twilio call, store call_sid, track recording
- AI response generator: webhook from workflow, call LLM (GPT-4 or Claude), generate next-action recommendation or SMS response, store in conversation
- Recording pipeline: receive Twilio recording URL, download to S3, trigger async transcription, link to conversation

**Workflow Engine**
- Trigger evaluation: on conversation event (call outcome, transcript analyzed), evaluate all active workflow conditions
- Condition matcher: check conversation_status, intent_detected array, contact tags, time window, crm field match (if integrated)
- Action dispatcher: for matched workflow, queue each action (call, sms, task, webhook) with execution order (sequential vs parallel)
- Rate limiter: enforce per-contact per-day execution limits; prevent spam; backoff on errors
- Retry mechanism: exponential backoff for transient failures; alert on repeated failure; skip if error_handling = skip

**Scheduling Engine**
- Cron job runner: evaluate reminders, sequences (next_step_due_at), scheduled workflows every 5 minutes
- Timezone-aware scheduling: convert org timezone to UTC, execute at correct local time
- Sequence step iterator: for each sequence_enrollment with due step, execute step action (call/sms/email), set next_step_due_at
- Reminder dispatcher: send SMS/email/in-app notification via delivery method; track sent_at, update status

**Follow-Up Engine**
- Missed-call recovery: on call_status = missed, create follow-up task, trigger missed-call workflow, send SMS/email reminder to contact
- No-show recovery: on booking_status = no_show, log event, trigger no-show workflow, attempt immediate recovery call, create task
- Appointment confirmation: on booking created, schedule reminder SMS/email 24h and 2h before
- Callback scheduling: on conversation outcome = callback_scheduled, create task, schedule reminder for assigned user

**Memory/Context Layer**
- Conversation history retriever: given contact_id, fetch last 10 conversations (calls, SMS, emails), summarize key intent/objections/outcomes
- Contact 360 view: aggregate all events, opportunities, tasks, notes for a contact; feed to AI for context-aware responses
- Industry context: if org industry = real_estate, preload relevant terminology, CRM field definitions, common objections
- Contact preferences cache: store preferred voice, contact window, language; invalidate on update

**Prioritization Layer**
- High-intent scoring: analyze conversation transcripts for keywords (interested, timeline, budget, authority); flag for rep attention
- Missed-call priority: score by contact value (opportunity stage/size), outcome (qualified vs cold), time since miss
- Lead scoring: if CRM integrated, fetch lead score; use for conversation routing and follow-up urgency
- No-show risk: predict contacts likely to cancel based on historical patterns; pro-active reminder

**Analytics Aggregation**
- Real-time event stream: Kafka or Bull queue, ingest all events (call, sms, workflow, conversion)
- Metric calculator: daily job aggregates response_speed, booked_appointments, recovery_rate, revenue_influenced; store in analytics_events
- Cohort builder: segment contacts by acquisition_date, industry, source; track conversion by cohort
- Funnel analyzer: track contact progression (initial contact → qualified → proposal → won); measure drop-off at each stage
- Churn predictor: ML model (optional) trained on historical data; flag high-risk accounts

**Billing Meter Events**
- Call metering: on call_ended, emit billing_event with duration_seconds, contact_id, conversation_id
- SMS metering: on sms_sent, emit billing_event with sms_count
- AI response metering: on ai_response generated, emit billing_event with token_count (estimate)
- Voice inference metering: on voice call initiated, start timer; on call_ended, emit voice_usage_record with inference_seconds, cost_usd
- Voice training metering: on training_job completed, emit billing_event with training_minutes, cost_usd
- Storage metering: daily job counts S3 objects; emit usage_record with storage_used_gb
- API call metering: middleware on /api/* routes counts request; daily batch emit
- Stripe Billing Meter sync: post events to Stripe Billing Meters API; Stripe calculates charges based on configured rates

**Cost-Tracking Hooks**
- Pre-action cost estimate: before workflow action (call, SMS, voice training), fetch estimated cost from Stripe Billing Meter config; compare against remaining budget; warn if over-quota
- Real-time cost aggregation: cache current month's costs; serve in billing dashboard; alert if approaching plan limit
- Cost per contact: track cumulative cost (calls + SMS + voice); flag high-cost contacts
- Cost per workflow: track cost of each active workflow; help identify inefficient sequences

**Queue Processing**
- Background job processor (Bull queue on Redis): voicemail transcription, sequence step execution, no-show recovery calls, reminder dispatch, data exports, analytics aggregation
- Job retry: 3 attempts with exponential backoff
- Job timeout: 5min for transcription, 10min for training, 1min for SMS/task creation
- Dead-letter queue: failed jobs after 3 retries; admin notification

**Admin Tooling**
- Org provisioning: create organization record, stripe customer, default billing_plan, sample templates, default voice profile
- User bulk import: CSV upload, parse email/name, batch create users, assign roles, send welcome emails
- Contact bulk import: CSV with phone/email/name/company, de-duplicate, validate consent, import to contacts table
- Data export: GDPR export all org data, generate CSV/JSON, zip, serve download
- Manual workflow trigger: admin UI to execute workflow on contact (for testing)
- Conversation replay: admin view to listen to call recording, read transcript, see all generated actions

**Observability**
- Structured logging (Winston): all requests, errors, background jobs log to stdout + Supabase (audit_logs table); include trace_id, user_id, org_id
- Error tracking (Sentry): capture exceptions, group by error type, alert on spike
- Performance monitoring (New Relic or custom): track API response time, database query time, workflow execution time; alert if p95 > 500ms
- Workflow execution metrics: track workflow trigger count, action execution count, success/failure rate per workflow
- Voice inference latency: track end-to-end latency (request → Fish Speech inference → audio return)

**Failure Handling**
- Transient failures (network timeouts): automatic retry with exponential backoff (1s, 2s, 4s, 8s)
- Vendor failures (Twilio down): queue call for retry; alert ops; use fallback provider if available
- Database failures: connection pool exhaustion → back off + alert; replicated DB → failover to replica
- Voice inference failure: log error, fallback to ElevenLabs or TTS fallback; notify ops
- Workflow error: log error, set workflow status to error, notify creator + admin; do not retry by default

**Vendor Abstraction Layer**
- Phone service interface: abstraction over Twilio; if Twilio fails, switch to bandwidth.com or Vonage; config-driven via environment
- SMS service interface: abstraction over Twilio SMS; fallback to AWS SNS; config-driven
- Voice TTS interface: abstraction over Fish Speech, ElevenLabs, fallback to built-in TTS (browser Web Audio)
- STT interface: abstraction over Faster-Whisper (self-hosted), fallback to Twilio transcription
- CRM sync interface: pluggable (Salesforce, HubSpot, Pipedrive); config via integration table

**Streaming Voice Pipeline**
- Audio capture: browser Web Audio API (MediaRecorder) or Twilio call stream
- Audio encoding: PCM 16kHz 16-bit mono
- Real-time STT: stream audio chunks to Faster-Whisper endpoint; receive partial transcripts via SSE
- Context injection: feed conversation history + contact 360 to LLM for intent detection + response generation in parallel with STT
- TTS response: stream generated text to Fish Speech; receive audio chunks; play back via Web Audio or Twilio
- Interruption handling: if user speaks while TTS playing, pause TTS, capture new audio, re-route

**Voice Training Jobs**
- Dataset upload: bulk upload .wav files; validate format + duration (min 5s, max 60s per file)
- Training request: queue job with dataset_id + target voice_profile_id
- Training worker: pull job from queue, call Fish Speech training API, monitor progress, save model_url to voice_version on completion
- Quality evaluation: post-training, run evaluation dataset (pre-recorded test prompts); compute MOS, WER; flag if below threshold (MOS < 3.5)
- Version activation: if quality passes, set is_production = true; make available for inference

**Voice Inference Service**
- Endpoint: POST /api/voice/:voice_profile_id/synthesize with body {text, speed, pitch}
- Routing: check if voice_profile is custom (is_custom_trained); if yes, use Fish Speech inference endpoint; else, use ElevenLabs or fallback
- Caching: hash text + voice_profile_id; check if audio cached in S3 voice_cache/; if hit, return URL; if miss, synthesize, cache, return
- Latency tracking: emit voice_usage_record with inference_seconds, latency_ms
- Error handling: if Fish Speech fails, fallback to ElevenLabs immediately; log error, alert ops

**Voice Routing Service**
- Assignment logic: when outbound call initiated, check contact.voice_profile_id; if null, use organization.default_voice_profile_id; if null, use system default
- A/B testing: if workflow has voice_profile_a_id and voice_profile_b_id, assign randomly 50/50; log assignment to conversation.metadata
- Consent verification: before using voice for contact, check voice_consents table; if no grant, use fallback voice or skip voice element
- Cost optimization: route high-frequency voices through cache; route rare voices through on-demand synthesis

**Consent Verification Service**
- Pre-workflow check: given contact_id, check voice_consents table; if none or all is_granted=false, do not queue voice-based actions
- Consent types: synthetic_voice (general), voice_profile_assignment (specific voice), voice_analytics (usage tracking)
- Bulk consent import: CSV with contact_phone + consent_type + is_granted; batch upsert voice_consents
- GDPR support: export all voice_consents for contact; delete on request; audit trail in audit_logs

---

## PART 4 — FRONTEND / UX REQUIREMENTS

### Onboarding Wizard
- Step 1: Organization name, industry, plan selection, trial length confirmation
- Step 2: Admin user email, password setup, verify email (link in inbox)
- Step 3: Logo upload, company address, billing email
- Step 4: Sample contact import or manual add first contact; guide through contact import CSV template
- Step 5: Select industry pack (if real_estate: include MLS fields, deal stage, commission templates); populate sample templates + sequences
- Step 6: Set up primary VCN phone number (Twilio); test outbound call
- Step 7: Choose default voice profile; customize (accent, speed, pitch); preview call with sample script
- Step 8: Set up integrations (CRM sync, Slack notifications)
- Step 9: Invite team members (email addresses); assign roles
- Step 10: Review dashboard; launch with sample workflow active

### Mode Selector (Top Navigation)
- Dropdown: Solo, Sales, Business
- Logic: if org has 1 team and 1 user → Auto-select Solo; if org has >1 user → default Sales; if multiple locations or advanced workflows → Business
- Persistence: store in user preferences; remember on next login
- Real-time indicator: show current mode pill; color-coded (solo=blue, sales=orange, business=purple)

### Dashboard System
- **Solo Dashboard**:
  - 4-box summary: Calls Booked Today, Pipeline Value (30-day), Revenue (30-day), Avg Response Speed
  - Quick actions row: New Contact, Start Call, Send SMS, View Inbox
  - Today's calls chart (call timeline, 6am-6pm)
  - Upcoming appointments (next 7 days)
  - Recent conversations (last 5, with outcome badge)
  
- **Sales Dashboard**:
  - 6-box summary: Leads This Week, Pipeline Value, Booked Appointments, Conversion Rate (%), Response Speed (avg min), Calls Made Today
  - Pipeline card: Kanban preview (prospects, qualified, proposal, closed), total value + deal count per stage
  - Team leaderboard (if team_id set): top 5 reps by calls_made, appointments_booked, conversion_rate
  - Call performance chart: calls over time (7d trend), success rate (booked vs not)
  - Opportunities by close date (calendar heat map)
  - Top workflows (most triggered this week)

- **Business Dashboard**:
  - Multi-org KPI grid: top organizations by revenue, calls, conversion
  - Location heat map: calls + revenue by location; top performers per location
  - Team health: active users, avg calls per user, team utilization %, churn risk (red flag accounts)
  - Financial summary: MRR, total calls, cost per call, gross margin %, forecast (if forecasting enabled)
  - Workflow efficiency: top workflows by ROI (revenue influenced / cost)
  - Budget status: current month spend vs. plan limit; cost per department/location

### Inbox UI
- 3-column layout: filters (left), conversation list (center), conversation detail (right)
- Filter options: by status (unread, active, completed, missed), channel (call, SMS, voicemail, email), priority (high-intent first), assigned_to_me, date range
- Conversation list: sorted by recency or priority; show contact name, last message preview, timestamp, channel icon, outcome badge (if completed)
- Conversation detail: full transcript (call) or message thread (SMS); action buttons (Mark Complete, Create Task, Log Outcome, Schedule Callback, Send SMS); notes field (editable); related opportunities + contacts
- Bulk actions: select multiple, mark complete, assign to user, add tag, delete
- Keyboard shortcuts: (J) next conversation, (K) prev, (C) mark complete, (T) create task

### Contact Timeline
- Vertical timeline: all events (calls, meetings, tasks, notes, status changes) in reverse chronological order
- Event cards: event type icon, brief summary, timestamp, actor name
- Detail popover: click event → see full details (call transcript, task description, note text)
- Add event: button to manually log call/email/meeting; quick form
- Notes section: editable, auto-save, @mention users for collaboration
- Related data: show linked opportunities, tasks, workflows
- Filters: by event type, date range, user

### Workflow Builder
- Canvas-based editor (React Flow): start node, trigger node(s), condition node(s), action node(s), end node
- Node types:
  - Trigger: conversation_outcome (passed dropdown: booking, callback, interested, no_action), event (e.g., appointment_no_show), scheduled (cron), webhook
  - Condition: conversation_intent_contains (dropdown: [interested, objection, not_interested]), conversation_status_is, contact_has_tag, date_is_in_window, custom_field_match
  - Action: make_call (contact selector, script selector), send_sms (template selector), send_email, create_task, update_opportunity, webhook_call, log_conversion
  - Logic: AND/OR gates, multiple conditions
- Configuration panel (right side): when node selected, show config form
- Validation: prevent incomplete nodes, highlight errors
- Preview: run workflow on sample contact, show dry-run results
- Publish: save, activate/deactivate toggle, version control (auto-increment on publish)
- Audit trail: show who created, last modified, when; rollback to previous version

### Sequence Builder
- Timeline-based editor: display steps in order (horizontally scrollable)
- Step card: action type (call/SMS/email), delay (hours/days), template selector, success criteria (dropdown)
- Add step: plus button between steps, modal to insert new step
- Branching (advanced): if contact.conversation_outcome = booking, skip remaining steps; if no response after 3 steps, trigger follow-up sequence
- A/B testing: toggle to enable, clone step A as step B, track variant metrics (conversion rate, response rate)
- Dry-run: simulate on sample contact, show projected timeline
- Publish: activate, set schedule (auto-enroll new contacts with matching tags, or manual trigger), view enrollments
- Performance metrics: conversion rate %, avg time to conversion, drop-off by step, best-performing variant

### Analytics / Reporting UI
- Tab navigation: Summary, Funnel, Cohort, Revenue, Team Performance, Custom
- **Summary tab**:
  - KPI cards: total calls, total SMS, total conversions, conversion rate %, missed-call recovery rate, no-show recovery rate, reactivation wins (count + value)
  - Response speed distribution: histogram (0-5min, 5-30min, 30-1h, 1h+)
  - Calls by outcome: pie chart (booked, callback, interested, no action, declined)
  - Revenue influenced: bar chart by month (last 6 months), cumulative trend line
  - Top contacts (by value + interaction count)
  - Top workflows (by conversion rate)
  
- **Funnel tab**:
  - Stage funnel (custom stages from org): initial contact → qualified → proposal → won; show drop-off %, average time per stage
  - Opportunity flow: source → stage progression → closed; identify bottleneck stages
  - Conversion by source: compare conversion rate for different contact sources
  
- **Cohort tab**:
  - Cohort selector: segment by industry, acquisition date range, contact source, team
  - Retention table: weeks/months since acquisition, retention % per cohort
  - Conversion table: cohort → conversion rate over time
  
- **Revenue tab**:
  - Revenue influenced: sum of opportunities moved to won/closed (attributed to recall touch)
  - Revenue recovered: sum of no-show recovery wins
  - Margin by location/team/rep
  - Forecast: if forecast enabled, show expected revenue (next 30/60/90 days)
  - LTV: avg lifetime value per contact
  
- **Team Performance tab**:
  - Leaderboard: rep name, calls made, appointments booked, conversion rate, revenue influenced
  - Comparison: select 2-3 reps, chart side-by-side (calls, conversion, avg deal size)
  - Activity heatmap: day of week + hour of day, color-coded by call volume
  
- **Custom tab**:
  - Report builder: drag/drop metrics, dimensions, filters
  - Export: download as CSV, PDF, Excel
  - Schedule delivery: email report weekly/monthly

### Billing/Usage UI
- Usage summary: current month calls (X/Y plan limit), SMS (X/Y), AI responses, voice minutes, storage
- Plan overview: current plan name, price, next renewal date, seat count
- Cost breakdown: calls ($X), SMS ($Y), voice training ($Z), total this month ($XXX)
- Upgrade/downgrade: button per available plan, show new price + features comparison
- Invoices: list of past invoices (date, amount, status, download PDF link)
- Add-ons: toggle switches for white-label, custom voice training (show price)
- Team seat management: current seat count, invite member (adds cost), remove member
- Billing contact: email, address (editable)
- Cost alerts: toggle to enable; set threshold (e.g., alert when month-to-date cost > 80% of plan budget)

### Team/Admin UI
- User list: name, email, role, team, last login, status (active/inactive)
- Add user: button, modal with email, role, team assignment
- Role editor: name, permissions checkboxes (contact.view, contact.create, report.view, etc.), save
- Bulk actions: select users, change role, change team, deactivate, send welcome email
- Activity audit: sortable table of user actions (login, create contact, edit workflow, etc.), timestamp, resource, changes
- Security: API key management (generate, revoke), IP whitelist, session management

### Integrations Hub
- Available integrations grid: CRM (Salesforce, HubSpot, Pipedrive), communication (Slack, Teams), automation (Zapier)
- Integration card: logo, description, status (connected/disconnected), setup button
- Setup flow: click setup, redirected to OAuth (if OAuth) or API key form; authorize, sync data, confirm success
- Sync status: show last sync time, sync frequency, error log (if failed)
- Disconnect: button to revoke access, clear cached data

### Template Gallery
- Browse: filter by type (SMS, email, call script, voicemail), category (initial_outreach, follow_up, recovery, closing), industry
- Preview: click card, see template content with sample variable values ({{first_name}} → "John")
- Use: button to copy to personal template library or apply to workflow
- Customize: open in template editor, modify content, save as new template
- Org templates: shared by team, show usage count

### Industry Adaptation
- On first login (or admin dashboard), show industry selector modal if not set
- Display: industry name, description, included custom fields (e.g., MLS for real_estate: property_address, list_price, days_on_market)
- Apply: button to apply industry pack; adds templates, sequences, voice profiles, workflow suggestions
- Customize: edit custom fields, reorder, map to CRM fields (if CRM integrated)

### Voice Library UI
- Voice profile list: name, provider (Fish Speech, ElevenLabs), gender, tone, language, quality_score (if trained)
- Preview button: play sample text ("Hello, this is a test message") with the voice
- Create new: button, modal with name, gender, accent, tone, speed, pitch sliders; assign to contacts/workflows
- Train custom voice: button, upload dataset (wav files), monitor training progress, quality evaluation, activate when ready
- Voice versions: if custom trained, show version history, metrics (MOS, WER), rollback option
- Pronunciation rules: list of term → pronunciation mappings; add/edit rules
- Default voice: set organization default; allow contact-level override
- Voice assignment: bulk assign voice to contacts by tag/segment

### Voice Preview
- Minimal UI: text input field, voice selector dropdown, play button
- Real-time synthesis: click play, stream audio from Fish Speech or ElevenLabs, play in browser
- Settings: speed slider (0.5-2.0), pitch slider (0.5-2.0), accent selector (if available)
- Sample scripts: dropdown with industry-relevant scripts (e.g., "Hello {{first_name}}, we found a property that might interest you")
- Save as favorite: star button to save custom script for quick access

### Pronunciation Editor
- Table view: term, pronunciation (phonetic), context example, priority, created_by
- Add rule: button, modal with term input, pronunciation input (with phonetic guide), context example, priority dropdown
- Test pronunciation: audio preview of term with pronunciation rule applied
- Bulk import: CSV with term + pronunciation; upload and import
- Applies to all voices: toggle to make rule global or voice-specific

### Voice Assignment Controls
- Contact detail view: voice profile selector dropdown (+ preview button)
- Workflow action editor: when action_type = call, show voice profile selector
- Sequence step editor: when step_action = call, show voice profile selector
- Bulk assignment: contact list, select multiple, dropdown to assign voice
